<a class="hotel_name_link url" data-et-click="
" href="/hotel/jp/green-rich-kyoto.zh-tw.html?label=gen173nr-1DCAEoggJCAlhYSDNiBW5vcmVmaOcBiAEBmAEwuAEGyAEM2AED6AEBkgIBeagCAw;sid=4996667e149bfae490c17f2eb37eafa9;checkin=2017-09-13;checkout=2017-09-17;ucfs=1;soh=1;srpvid=ac42264088ed0222;highlighted_blocks=;all_sr_blocks=;room1=A%2CA;soldout=0%2C0;hpos=11;dest_type=city;dest_id=-235402;srfid=d394b490e3906885ad4aef45c338eb3239ec3ce0X261;from=searchresults;highlight_room=#hotelTmpl" rel="noopener" target="_blank">

<span class="invisible_spoken">3 星級飯店</span></i>

<span class="invisible_spoken">此住宿已同意參與我們的首選住宿計畫。首選住宿以優惠價格為顧客提供最卓越且具高性價比的服務。參與此計畫的住宿業者必須符合特定標準，曾入住顧客之意見亦會納入評估考量。</span></i>
